## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Event["Incoming AWS Lambda Event"] -->|headers/requestContext| Decorators["Decorators applied\n(add_reference -> set_request_id -> set_lambda_id -> set_lambda_level)"]
    Decorators --> Sanitized["sanitize(event)"]
    Sanitized --> LogEvent["log_event(event)"]
    LogEvent --> ParseBody{"get_event_body(event)\nstring->json?"}
    ParseBody --> Schema{"schema_validation_v2 or schema_validation"}
    Schema --> AuthCheck{"prepare_auth & auth.check_auth_wrapper\n(if auth_check present)"}
    AuthCheck --> Business["Lambda handler logic (f)"]
    Business --> Response{"res returned"}
    Response --> SizeCheck{"pickle size check > 5MB?"}
    SizeCheck -- yes --> OverflowCheck{"fv-overflow header set?"}
    OverflowCheck -- yes --> SendToBucket["send_to_bucket -> presigned URL\nmake_response(SEE_OTHER)"]
    OverflowCheck -- no --> ErrorLargeBody["raise HandledException"]
    SizeCheck -- no --> Finalize["final response returned"]
    Business -->|exceptions| ErrorHandler["exception caught -> make_error_response"]
    Finalize --> AuditCheck{"to_audit(event,context)?"}
    AuditCheck -- yes --> requestAudit["invoke_lambda('request_audit', Event) or request_audit()"]
    requestAudit --> Done[("Return response to caller")]
    ErrorHandler --> Done
```

    subgraph EXPORT_FLOW

        S3Write --> Presigned["generate_presigned_url"]
        Presigned --> UpdateDB["update_s3_content_processing(status, uuid, presigned_url, user_id)"]
        UpdateDB --> Notify["create_notification -> invoke_lambda('create_notification')"]
        Notify --> ReturnID["return identifier"]
    end

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Client
    participant Lambda as Handler
    participant Auth as AuthModule
    participant S3
    participant SNS
    participant DB
    Client->>Lambda: invoke event
    Lambda->>Auth: prepare_auth / check_auth_wrapper
    Auth-->>Lambda: privileges ok / error
    Lambda->>Lambda: get_event_body(), schema_validation_v2()
    Lambda->>S3: upload exported file (csv/pdf)
    S3-->>Lambda: presigned_url
    Lambda->>DB: insert/update process_s3_content (uuid,status,presigned_url)
    Lambda->>SNS: invoke create_notification (via invoke_lambda)
    SNS-->>Lambda: publish result
    Lambda-->>Client: return presigned_url or identifier
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Idle
    Idle --> Receiving : event arrives
    Receiving --> Sanitizing : sanitize(event)
    Sanitizing --> Validating : schema_validation / auth
    Validating --> Executing : handler execution
    Executing --> Success : returns res
    Executing --> Error : exception thrown
    Error --> ErrorHandling : make_error_response -> send_exception
    Success --> Auditing : to_audit? -> request_audit
    Auditing --> [*] : finished
    ErrorHandling --> Auditing : (may still audit)
    ErrorHandling --> [*] : finished
```
